namespace $ {

  export class Store extends $mol_object {
    
    @ $mol_mem
    static yard() {
      return new $hyoo_sync_client
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    static home() {
      return this.yard().world().home()
    }
    
  }

  export class Entity< Schema > extends $mol_store< Schema > {

    id(): $mol_int62_string {
      return '0_0'
    }

    head(): $mol_int62_string {
      return '0_0'
    }
    
    @ $mol_mem
    land() {
      return Store.yard().land( this.id() )
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    state() {
      return this.land().node( this.head(), $hyoo_crowd_struct )
    }
    
  }

  interface Schema {
    name?: string, // $hyoo_crowd_reg
    flag?: boolean, // $hyoo_crowd_reg
    age?: number, // $hyoo_crowd_reg
    avatar?: Blob, // $hyoo_crowd_blob
    cities: string[], // $hyoo_crowd_list
    flags?: boolean[],
    ages?: number[],
    images?: Blob[], // $hyoo_crowd_list + $hyoo_crowd_blob
    options?: { label: string, value: number }[], // $hyoo_crowd_list
    dict?: Map<string, string>, // $hyoo_crowd_dict
    post?: $hyoo_crowd_text,
  }

  export class Person extends Entity<Schema> {
    // –ß–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å/–ü–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –≤ —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —É–∂–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã—Ç—å –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∏–Ω—Ç—Å–∞–Ω—Å—É
    // const obj = new Person
    // obj.value('name', 'Thomas')
    // –î–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—É—é –ª–æ–≥–∏–∫—É –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è–µ–º –≤ —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞—Ö
  }

}

ARG REG
ARG SRV=demo
ARG NODE=20
ARG NGINX=1

FROM ${REG}/dhub/library/node:${NODE} as node
ARG SRV=demo
ARG APP=gd/${SRV}
ARG MAM=/mam

# fix npx mam ... & npm need self update:
RUN npm install -g npm mam

RUN git clone https://github.com/hyoo-ru/mam.git ${MAM}
WORKDIR ${MAM}
RUN npm install

# for cache all deps clone:
RUN npm start mol/icon

COPY . ${MAM}/${APP}
RUN npm start ${APP}


FROM ${REG}/dhub/library/nginx:${NGINX}
ARG SRV=demo
ARG APP=gd/${SRV}
ARG MAM=/mam

COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf
COPY --from=node ${MAM}/${APP}/-/ /usr/share/nginx/html

include: .gitlab-ci/*.yml

workflow:
  rules:
    - if: $CI_COMMIT_MESSAGE =~ /noci/
      when: never
    - when: always

variables:
  _K: /root/.kube/config

stages:
  - build
  - deploy

default:
  image: $REG/dhub/library/docker:24.0.4-cli
  tags:
    - kube-runner

demo-build:
  stage: build
  tags:
    - buildx
  script:
    - cd demo &&
      source .env &&
      docker buildx build --push -t $REG/gd/$SRV:$RT
      --build-arg REG=$REG
      --build-arg SRV=$SRV
      --build-arg NODE=$NODE
      --build-arg NGINX=$NGINX
      --platform linux/arm64/v8,linux/amd64 .
  only:
    changes:
      - demo/.env

demo-deploy:
  stage: deploy
  environment:
    name: "ref/$CI_COMMIT_REF_SLUG"
  image: $REG/ci/helmwave:0.29.3
  variables:
    GIT_SUBMODULE_STRATEGY: "normal" # https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/ci/git_submodules.html git submodule add --name gd-ci ../gd-ci.git
    GIT_DEPTH: "2" # https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/ci/runners/configure_runners.html#shallow-cloning
    HELMWAVE_TEMPLATER: gomplate
    HELMWAVE_AUTO_BUILD: "true"
    HELMWAVE_AUTO_YML: "true"
    HELMWAVE_KUBEDOG_ENABLED: "true"
    HELMWAVE_DIFF_SHOW_SECRET: "false"
    APP: demo
  script:
    - source $APP/.env && echo APP=$APP RT=$RT
    - cp $KUBE_CONFIG $_K
    - cd gd-ci && V=$RT helmwave up -t $APP
  artifacts:
    paths:
      - gd-ci/.helmwave
    expire_in: 1 week
  only:
    variables:
      - $KUBE_CONFIG
    changes:
      - demo/.env
      - gd-ci
      - .gitlab-ci.yml

@ $mol_mem
messages(next?: Array<InstanceType<typeof Message>>) {
    return next ?? []
}

@ $mol_mem_key
Message( id: string ) {
    return new Message
}

@ $mol_action
create_message( id: string, msg: string ) {
    const obj = this.Message(id)
    obj.text(msg)
    this.messages( [...this.messages(), obj ]) 
}

–∞, —ç—Ç–æ –≤ —Å–æ–≤—Å–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–π –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏–∏


  const store = new Map

  /** Returns room attached to origin */
  function Room( origin ) {

    let room = store.get( origin )
    
    if( !room ) {
      store.set( origin, room = {
        watch: new Map,
        cache: new Map,
      } )
    }
    
    return room
  }


  /** Returns value by keys and subscribes line to value cahnges */
  async function get( origin, key, line ) {
    
    const room = Room( origin )

    if( line ) {

      let keys = room.watch.get( line )
      if( !keys ) room.watch.set( line, keys = new Set )
      
      keys.add( key )
    }

    let val = room.cache.get( key )
    if( val !== undefined ) return val
    
    let res = db.query(`SELECT value FROM store WHERE key = $1::text`, [ origin + '/' + key ] )
    room.cache.set( key, res )
    res = await res

    val = res.rows[0] ? res.rows[0].value.delta : null
    room.cache.set( key, val )

    return val
  }


  /** Unsubscribes line from all keys */
  function forget( origin, line ) {
    const room = Room( origin )
    room.watch.delete( line )
  }

 .on( 'close', ( code, reason )=> {
      forget( origin, line )
    } )
